function related_results_labels_thumbs(json) {
for (var i = 0; i < json.feed.entry.length; i++) {
var entry = json.feed.entry[i];
relatedTitles[relatedTitlesNum] = entry.title.$t;
try 
{thumburl[relatedTitlesNum]=entry.media$thumbnail.url;}


catch (error){

s=entry.content.$t;a=s.indexOf("<img");b=s.indexOf("src=\"",a);c=s.indexOf("\"",b+5);d=s.substr(b+5,c-b-5);
if((a!=-1)&&(b!=-1)&&(c!=-1)&&(d!=""))
{thumburl[relatedTitlesNum]=d;} else {if(typeof(defaultnoimage) !== 'undefined') thumburl[relatedTitlesNum]=defaultnoimage; else thumburl[relatedTitlesNum]="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhz9Sd11Pv1mwiOvuwuEBe4q5DVoUukINlaIe2vzAQUSftT2dd5OIvpPhyphenhyphentMSgZFQKHeWbv_CZlAaeq8fYPRx7c2UZOt1mVRnTE6mkEz8i7HscIuS3P06Wd_XE2HKXbI8xdFSKImnRPQdb4/s1600/no-image-found.jpg";}

}

if(relatedTitles[relatedTitlesNum].length>35) relatedTitles[relatedTitlesNum]=relatedTitles[relatedTitlesNum].substring(0, 35)+"...";
for (var k = 0; k < entry.link.length; k++) {
if (entry.link[k].rel == 'alternate') {
relatedUrls[relatedTitlesNum] = entry.link[k].href;
relatedTitlesNum++;


}
}
}
}
function removeRelatedDuplicates_thumbs() {
var tmp = new Array(0);
var tmp2 = new Array(0);
var tmp3 = new Array(0);
for(var i = 0; i < relatedUrls.length; i++) {
if(!contains_thumbs(tmp, relatedUrls[i])) 
{
tmp.length += 1;
tmp[tmp.length - 1] = relatedUrls[i];
tmp2.length += 1;
tmp3.length += 1;
tmp2[tmp2.length - 1] = relatedTitles[i];
tmp3[tmp3.length - 1] = thumburl[i];
}
}
relatedTitles = tmp2;
relatedUrls = tmp;
thumburl=tmp3;


}
function contains_thumbs(a, e) {
for(var j = 0; j < a.length; j++) if (a[j]==e) return true;
return false;
}
function printRelatedLabels_thumbs(current) {
for(var i = 0; i < relatedUrls.length; i++)
{
if((relatedUrls[i]==current)||(!relatedTitles[i]))
{
relatedUrls.splice(i,1);
relatedTitles.splice(i,1);
thumburl.splice(i,1);
i--;
}
}


var r = Math.floor((relatedTitles.length - 1) * Math.random());
var i = 0;

while (i < relatedTitles.length && i < 20 && i<maxresults) {
tmb = thumburl[r].replace('s72-c/','s300-c/');

document.write('<div class="item-related"><a href="' + relatedUrls[r] + '"><img width="150" height="100" src="'+tmb+'"/></a><h3><a href="' + relatedUrls[r] + '">'+relatedTitles[r]+'</a></h3></div>');i++;


if (r < relatedTitles.length - 1) {
r++;
} else {
r = 0;
}

}

relatedUrls.splice(0,relatedUrls.length);
thumburl.splice(0,thumburl.length);
relatedTitles.splice(0,relatedTitles.length);

}
function removeHtmlTag(strx, chop) {
    var s = strx.split("<");
    for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
        if (s[i].indexOf(">") != -1) {
            s[i] = s[i].substring(s[i].indexOf(">") + 1, s[i].length)
        }
    }
    s = s.join("");
    s = s.substring(0, chop - 1);
    return s
}

      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiXJqL4Kz7RAF8ITmKGwhfEDTDHpj8-kL6VRF3XJ_9inuKBBmBlqzK-Ilvb3leiG3cpKRpGA5gRCpl_yi2l5K_3UGSkjXIIVecds-iZxo8IwNndQ7RRpacHV_YlBxQAO2dzzgsCSYajNhmh5THAOu03AI5Mppst1JWvhhXBB4Y7rx3IWt1MIYbmw29JEg0k/s3857/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_12.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Iffa Chicken, chicken iffa, viral Dubai style iffa chicken, viral Dubai style chicken iffa, viral Dubai recipe, food, fusion food, food blog,  food content creator, recipe, comfort food, smoked chicken, indian cuisine, south asian cuisine, middle eastern cusion, food blogger, chicken recipe, chicken and rice, chicken and naan, chicken and roti, roti, rice, naan, saucy chicken, kashmiri red chilli powder, creamy white sauce, high protein, spicy food, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, pinterest food, Dubai style, google pixel, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3857" data-original-width="2893" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiXJqL4Kz7RAF8ITmKGwhfEDTDHpj8-kL6VRF3XJ_9inuKBBmBlqzK-Ilvb3leiG3cpKRpGA5gRCpl_yi2l5K_3UGSkjXIIVecds-iZxo8IwNndQ7RRpacHV_YlBxQAO2dzzgsCSYajNhmh5THAOu03AI5Mppst1JWvhhXBB4Y7rx3IWt1MIYbmw29JEg0k/w480-h640/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_12.jpg" title="Iffa Chicken" width="480"></a></div></span><br>
  <div data-end="387" data-start="0" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">I came across this <i>Viral Dubai-style</i> <b>Iffa Chicken</b>&#160;on my explore page, and I couldn&#39;t resist adding my own twist to it and giving it a
      try. It was so delicious, t</span><span style="font-family: arial;">hat I
      immediately moved it up my posting schedule.&#160;</span></div>
  <div data-end="387" data-start="0" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;
      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi1ktuDq4ev5-8ZWjyo14fxiruXivaJB-jpYWJIPFcQbCsb6_KgcIPhp754UVDYlqFarbhovFrQ4RAzAvzv5RljM-6rPS6iYbC7OJFh7pvhRh5sR8Qs9eqSzRhDweBSILMheSfnMZvBx-BmxDzHT2gGmSgZd5_7sWWizMFS_bnworAbbReSJ3q9PzTDWBRp/s3790/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_32.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Iffa Chicken, chicken iffa, viral Dubai style iffa chicken, viral Dubai style chicken iffa, viral Dubai recipe, food, fusion food, food blog,  food content creator, recipe, comfort food, smoked chicken, indian cuisine, south asian cuisine, middle eastern cusion, food blogger, chicken recipe, chicken and rice, chicken and naan, chicken and roti, roti, rice, naan, saucy chicken, kashmiri red chilli powder, creamy white sauce, high protein, spicy food, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, pinterest food, Dubai style, google pixel, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3790" data-original-width="2850" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi1ktuDq4ev5-8ZWjyo14fxiruXivaJB-jpYWJIPFcQbCsb6_KgcIPhp754UVDYlqFarbhovFrQ4RAzAvzv5RljM-6rPS6iYbC7OJFh7pvhRh5sR8Qs9eqSzRhDweBSILMheSfnMZvBx-BmxDzHT2gGmSgZd5_7sWWizMFS_bnworAbbReSJ3q9PzTDWBRp/w482-h640/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_32.jpg" title="Iffa Chicken" width="482"></a>
      </div>
      <br></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="855" data-start="389" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">This recipe draws inspiration from South Asian and Middle Eastern
      flavours, combining a spiced yoghurt-marinated chicken base with a rich,
      creamy topping and a signature charcoal smoke finish. The traditional
      <i data-end="620" data-start="611">smoking&#160;</i>method gives it that
      unmistakable restaurant-style aroma without needing an outdoor grill. It&#39;s
      comfort food with flair.</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="855" data-start="389" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1255" data-start="857" style="text-align: center;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEj3qGjZAS2xTGRjtD2hjHC4grRhUt2tvdRGVi-cs957dI-Sti3vgWIy3Oydh94bUXFNnhK2phmVyeGurHY1BZyu0lwPLUmh5e60oLUCTz8o5LTxcaOkwFKMwbbH2bmX146IJZGDBsikmNjJceRWp9rVt2eHOhtrN9mYefASfm0fW6-qcKmvjRslOSSmS3yO/s4080/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_35.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Iffa Chicken, chicken iffa, viral Dubai style iffa chicken, viral Dubai style chicken iffa, viral Dubai recipe, food, fusion food, food blog,  food content creator, recipe, comfort food, smoked chicken, indian cuisine, south asian cuisine, middle eastern cusion, food blogger, chicken recipe, chicken and rice, chicken and naan, chicken and roti, roti, rice, naan, saucy chicken, kashmiri red chilli powder, creamy white sauce, high protein, spicy food, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, pinterest food, Dubai style, google pixel, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4080" data-original-width="3072" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEj3qGjZAS2xTGRjtD2hjHC4grRhUt2tvdRGVi-cs957dI-Sti3vgWIy3Oydh94bUXFNnhK2phmVyeGurHY1BZyu0lwPLUmh5e60oLUCTz8o5LTxcaOkwFKMwbbH2bmX146IJZGDBsikmNjJceRWp9rVt2eHOhtrN9mYefASfm0fW6-qcKmvjRslOSSmS3yO/w482-h640/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_35.jpg" title="Iffa Chicken" width="482"></a>
      </div>
      <br></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1658" data-start="1257" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">Now let&#39;s talk about the <b>Creamy White Sauce</b>, because I know the
      <i>boiled egg</i> ingredient might raise an eyebrow. As someone who isn&#39;t fond of boiled eggs, I was pleasantly surprised. The sauce
      blends into a smooth, luscious topping with
      <u>no noticeable eggy smell or taste</u> whatsoever. Instead, it adds body
      and richness, creating a beautifully balanced finish that ties the entire
      dish together.</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1658" data-start="1257" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;
      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi8x-YL45AtPEI4isL2qJRndXKrTNRPd9sUqxPFIyxaBy7mQzAl-30rO4tkxM4P8jLRs9DR-6-wLfJpCJMwTPWZbkW_tbm-Rk1t_XXM7mNnew60FI2n_3X0_CJc5l-EiSHoDzdTMVFO601LR-oOjUM88usrPNmkJdHDI9vf6Z3VtMJIvrgN7bKlMEKy9rSO/s4064/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_19.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Iffa Chicken, chicken iffa, viral Dubai style iffa chicken, viral Dubai style chicken iffa, viral Dubai recipe, food, fusion food, food blog,  food content creator, recipe, comfort food, smoked chicken, indian cuisine, south asian cuisine, middle eastern cusion, food blogger, chicken recipe, chicken and rice, chicken and naan, chicken and roti, roti, rice, naan, saucy chicken, kashmiri red chilli powder, creamy white sauce, high protein, spicy food, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, pinterest food, Dubai style, google pixel, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi8x-YL45AtPEI4isL2qJRndXKrTNRPd9sUqxPFIyxaBy7mQzAl-30rO4tkxM4P8jLRs9DR-6-wLfJpCJMwTPWZbkW_tbm-Rk1t_XXM7mNnew60FI2n_3X0_CJc5l-EiSHoDzdTMVFO601LR-oOjUM88usrPNmkJdHDI9vf6Z3VtMJIvrgN7bKlMEKy9rSO/w482-h640/IffaChicken_DubaiViral_SFK_2026_19.jpg" title="Iffa Chicken" width="482"></a>
      </div>
      <br></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1949" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="1660" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: arial;">This viral chicken recipe genuinely lives up to
      expectations, and is absolutely worth trying.
      With simple ingredients you have in the kitchen, it&#39;s easy to prep and
      cook. Can be served with roti, naan or rice.</span>
  </div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>

  </div>
  <h2 style="text-align: center;">
    <span style="font-family: Great Vibes; font-size: x-large;">&#160;</span>
  </h2>
  <h2 style="text-align: center;">
    <span style="font-family: Great Vibes; font-size: x-large;">&quot;Honey buns from Honey&#39;s bakery...&quot;&#160;</span>
  </h2>
  <h2 style="text-align: center;">
    <span style="font-family: Great Vibes; font-size: x-large;">&#160;</span>
  </h2>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;"></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
  <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgVezlSd1C_4FG42OIGOBm72BY7xYTtCHJT1d5ueLeqOSAk8oE2VWamITAVxOFywuPAVwudFmlTmXxmnDImOTHa0ADfnshWFKiSgJyesWMtZuO07Hj0xhKACv8sDrr8x4bEtdGut24rVm74Y5fX6lB6taxccMr_B_hTMz8JrYQCFUvz5TxYLw_FPFfW8Yxv/s3840/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_42.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Honeycomb Bread, Yemeni Honeycomb Bread, Khaliat al Nahl, Khaliat Nahl, Middle-Eastern Bread, Middle-Eastern recipe, sweet bread, Yemeni Khaliat Nahl, brunch, tea table, food, foodie food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, recipe reel, recipe video, baking, bread, ramadan, eid, cream cheese, honey buns, finger food, sweet, google pixel, foodflatlay, orange cat, honey, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3840" data-original-width="2160" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgVezlSd1C_4FG42OIGOBm72BY7xYTtCHJT1d5ueLeqOSAk8oE2VWamITAVxOFywuPAVwudFmlTmXxmnDImOTHa0ADfnshWFKiSgJyesWMtZuO07Hj0xhKACv8sDrr8x4bEtdGut24rVm74Y5fX6lB6taxccMr_B_hTMz8JrYQCFUvz5TxYLw_FPFfW8Yxv/w360-h640/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_42.jpg" title="Honeycomb Bread (Khaliat Al Nahl)" width="360"></a>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;"><br></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <div data-end="404" data-start="0" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">Staring off Ramadan with
      <i>one of&#160;my&#160;favourite sweet treats in the entire world</i><b>,</b>&#160;<b>Honeycomb Bread (Khaliat Al Nahl)</b>. With absolutely
      no shame, if left alone with a full tray, I can (and will) finish the
      whole lot by myself. They are&#160;<i>outrageously addictive</i>.</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="404" data-start="0" style="text-align: center;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;
      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEh3wRuh0B8yQEfX1WVvOtQXPqmmIlExYI4Zn58ATZuv3C4jupvQEyrbrEggLvh4yHAm-dgU4BEc5tTXM6JN963h7py-ZGdgRap_Ozx_GbKK2bzlR-tzJ5d2udu2ptU43Ld7H826ayHP74Ti9D8TLYdv1SLm3rtkzfT3ITe-wTkeNq_YVikpDlM-tc5KnOYi/s4064/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_33.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Honeycomb Bread, Yemeni Honeycomb Bread, Khaliat al Nahl, Khaliat Nahl, Middle-Eastern Bread, Middle-Eastern recipe, sweet bread, Yemeni Khaliat Nahl, brunch, tea table, food, foodie food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, recipe reel, recipe video, baking, bread, ramadan, eid, cream cheese, honey buns, finger food, sweet, google pixel, foodflatlay, orange cat, honey, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEh3wRuh0B8yQEfX1WVvOtQXPqmmIlExYI4Zn58ATZuv3C4jupvQEyrbrEggLvh4yHAm-dgU4BEc5tTXM6JN963h7py-ZGdgRap_Ozx_GbKK2bzlR-tzJ5d2udu2ptU43Ld7H826ayHP74Ti9D8TLYdv1SLm3rtkzfT3ITe-wTkeNq_YVikpDlM-tc5KnOYi/w482-h640/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_33.jpg" title="Honeycomb Bread (Khaliat Al Nahl)" width="482"></a>
      </div>
      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <br></div></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="845" data-start="406" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">Originally from the <b>Middle East</b>, this bread is traditionally known
      as <i data-end="493" data-start="476">Khaliat Al Nahl</i> (خلية النحل),
      which literally translates to &quot;beehive&quot;. The name couldn&#39;t be more
      fitting, with its pull-apart rolls nestled together like <i>honeycomb</i>.
      It is often referred to as Yemeni Honeycomb Bread, and through friends, I
      came to know just how popular it is in Tanzania.</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="845" data-start="406" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="845" data-start="406" style="text-align: center;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhu4XaWWh8ZB6FPmbngTxX5Lh90Sf3I62zJQWoBrto01WPQVXvRCDub_cvRyKFCeu_f0-a5gublIYnAbeNK-Di-CeiaeyyF1bF3OyEQloGYJZ-S0KmMuLz4QiUYjqQmos1D0zm0OMNDO_LfwWRn2t1vfvYUiz27hprjGjSSz3KdHa5TA5eV2c3jAMAaMt_m/s3849/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_08.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Honeycomb Bread, Yemeni Honeycomb Bread, Khaliat al Nahl, Khaliat Nahl, Middle-Eastern Bread, Middle-Eastern recipe, sweet bread, Yemeni Khaliat Nahl, brunch, tea table, food, foodie food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, recipe reel, recipe video, baking, bread, ramadan, eid, cream cheese, honey buns, finger food, sweet, google pixel, foodflatlay, orange cat, honey, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3849" data-original-width="2887" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhu4XaWWh8ZB6FPmbngTxX5Lh90Sf3I62zJQWoBrto01WPQVXvRCDub_cvRyKFCeu_f0-a5gublIYnAbeNK-Di-CeiaeyyF1bF3OyEQloGYJZ-S0KmMuLz4QiUYjqQmos1D0zm0OMNDO_LfwWRn2t1vfvYUiz27hprjGjSSz3KdHa5TA5eV2c3jAMAaMt_m/w480-h640/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_08.jpg" title="Honeycomb Bread (Khaliat Al Nahl)" width="480"></a>
      </div>
      <br></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1250" data-start="847" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">Classically, honeycomb bread is finished with a
      <u>warm honey syrup</u> poured generously over the top, soaking into every
      crevice. Across different cultures, though, people have had a little fun
      with it, <u>condensed milk</u> being a particularly popular twist.
      Naturally, I couldn&#39;t resist combining the two. Honey
      <i data-end="1154" data-start="1149">and</i> condensed milk over soft
      bread with a cream cheese filling just felt like the right life
      choice.</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1250" data-start="847" style="text-align: center;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;
      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhaexa84Glbr6f5a0uGPtjuUYE2jr_p7WA5-FxyxHelQ4KIj_4SYFAJ5tpS6z9s0PfC2OkrIsqkc38zfivMQcmZBLAatF3Z6tzAobv5dwpKod0W4W-V4IHDCMVhiW0tZlw8ptIEpYDK-zqsqRHwIHi-H4mU1qNJrpt5MrKsDIaYG_05CEGWELwy3DAcTUDD/s1920/HoneycomBread_SFK_2026_00.webp" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Honeycomb Bread, Yemeni Honeycomb Bread, Khaliat al Nahl, Khaliat Nahl, Middle-Eastern Bread, Middle-Eastern recipe, sweet bread, Yemeni Khaliat Nahl, brunch, tea table, food, foodie food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, recipe reel, recipe video, baking, bread, ramadan, eid, cream cheese, honey buns, finger food, sweet, google pixel, foodflatlay, orange cat, honey, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="1920" data-original-width="1080" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhaexa84Glbr6f5a0uGPtjuUYE2jr_p7WA5-FxyxHelQ4KIj_4SYFAJ5tpS6z9s0PfC2OkrIsqkc38zfivMQcmZBLAatF3Z6tzAobv5dwpKod0W4W-V4IHDCMVhiW0tZlw8ptIEpYDK-zqsqRHwIHi-H4mU1qNJrpt5MrKsDIaYG_05CEGWELwy3DAcTUDD/w360-h640/HoneycomBread_SFK_2026_00.webp" title="Honeycomb Bread (Khaliat Al Nahl)" width="360"></a>
      </div>
      <br></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1868" data-start="1252" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">Those who follow me on my social media will know my cat,&#160;<i>Honey,</i>
      well and that I called him&#160;<b>Honey Buns</b>. He&#160;was always BTS,
      right in the middle of my kitchen storms and recipe shoots, meowing away
      like the boss he was. Whenever I saw him kneading on the blanket like he
      was hard at work, he would say,
      <i>&quot;Honey&#39;s making honey buns for Honey&#39;s Bakery.&quot;</i>&#160;</span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1868" data-start="1252" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;
      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhx7bLra4lNRm9o8zPR2IxtWTJOu6jEeBEdIIWVTpScDFeEovqDK2MEUF4I9v87kpPQ4OKVkpPQAwB5e5mPG3DdAgaSv6aJS4VV8QhlFI1yHX-d46ND0qEBfVcZJQOWKniYlYEl8s3vY4Tb3t28Jzu8iR5Y6fuxFETPZabbge3h4i-x2rgxsTsCCZoM0IbA/s4080/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_07.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Honeycomb Bread, Yemeni Honeycomb Bread, Khaliat al Nahl, Khaliat Nahl, Middle-Eastern Bread, Middle-Eastern recipe, sweet bread, Yemeni Khaliat Nahl, brunch, tea table, food, foodie food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, recipe reel, recipe video, baking, bread, ramadan, eid, cream cheese, honey buns, finger food, sweet, google pixel, foodflatlay, orange cat, honey, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4080" data-original-width="3072" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhx7bLra4lNRm9o8zPR2IxtWTJOu6jEeBEdIIWVTpScDFeEovqDK2MEUF4I9v87kpPQ4OKVkpPQAwB5e5mPG3DdAgaSv6aJS4VV8QhlFI1yHX-d46ND0qEBfVcZJQOWKniYlYEl8s3vY4Tb3t28Jzu8iR5Y6fuxFETPZabbge3h4i-x2rgxsTsCCZoM0IbA/w482-h640/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_07.jpg" title="Honeycomb Bread (Khaliat Al Nahl)" width="482"></a>
      </div>
      <br></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1868" data-start="1252" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">While I am endlessly grateful for the ten years Allah (God) blessed me
      with him, I still really miss him, and Ramadan without him won&#39;t feel the
      same. The <b>little paw print pressed into the dough</b> with Nigella
      Seeds<i><b> </b></i><b>i</b><b>s my quiet nod to my forever sweet golden boy.</b></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="1868" data-start="1252" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;&#160;
      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjDVhbfWMMaKy7ay4biRtUmg0cH_AGmMxqPKzKEfsWgIPqZ_hS9rAr82rux-u5XYDzmbUUWXg5481qtdY8MjvC0DbgUm9eublWlOUG1I_VWpYptGkj3iSx0mD8CsNJYoH_QoMADWXV_gBg4ST-xd8QPl4TJPUT71ami8wCY3mDB6XiXT3qzCqGs-HhuySm9/s4064/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_22.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Honeycomb Bread, Yemeni Honeycomb Bread, Khaliat al Nahl, Khaliat Nahl, Middle-Eastern Bread, Middle-Eastern recipe, sweet bread, Yemeni Khaliat Nahl, brunch, tea table, food, foodie food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, recipe reel, recipe video, baking, bread, ramadan, eid, cream cheese, honey buns, finger food, sweet, google pixel, foodflatlay, orange cat, honey, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjDVhbfWMMaKy7ay4biRtUmg0cH_AGmMxqPKzKEfsWgIPqZ_hS9rAr82rux-u5XYDzmbUUWXg5481qtdY8MjvC0DbgUm9eublWlOUG1I_VWpYptGkj3iSx0mD8CsNJYoH_QoMADWXV_gBg4ST-xd8QPl4TJPUT71ami8wCY3mDB6XiXT3qzCqGs-HhuySm9/w482-h640/HoneycombBread_SFK_2025_22.jpg" title="Honeycomb Bread (Khaliat Al Nahl)" width="482"></a>
      </div>
      <br></span>
  </div>
  <div data-end="2244" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="1870" style="text-align: left;">
    <span style="font-family: arial;">These are best served warm or hot, when the cream cheese is soft, and the
      glaze melts beautifully into the bread. They
      <u>reheat perfectly in the microwave</u>, making them ideal for make-ahead
      treats. You can also <u>meal prep</u> them, freeze them, and thaw for
      another day, just warm them through and pour the sweet glaze over the top.
      Fresh, comforting, and indulgent every single time.&#160;</span>
  </div>
</div>

    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><br></div></span>
  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
    <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhlGICWLn3RELqB7A5vnAmQEc7TzZ0e0lgKMqQBfrTETiphIfPOz-BtlbS41ViQ97Vj4QYPMBR4gqgrjWgxweORrqhY9csLIQVnGX7SW7-gdbbwcp72lO3Me-qqPOw4XNajp6LexAPkrxJG0ouXJ4pgu0d6PMsYywaZPsPwGpJlcTXP23_v3XDE2RVK74EG/s4064/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_40.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Chicken Fajita Pasta, chicken pasta, creamy pasta, creamy chicken pasta, fajita pasta, chicken recipe, pasta, pasta recipe,  food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food flatlay, one pot recipe, meal plan, google pixel, spicy food, spicy pasta, easy pasta, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhlGICWLn3RELqB7A5vnAmQEc7TzZ0e0lgKMqQBfrTETiphIfPOz-BtlbS41ViQ97Vj4QYPMBR4gqgrjWgxweORrqhY9csLIQVnGX7SW7-gdbbwcp72lO3Me-qqPOw4XNajp6LexAPkrxJG0ouXJ4pgu0d6PMsYywaZPsPwGpJlcTXP23_v3XDE2RVK74EG/w482-h640/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_40.jpg" style="outline: red dashed 1px;" title="Chicken Fajita Pasta" width="482"></a>
  </div>
</div>
<h2 data-end="382" data-start="0" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: Satisfy; font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: x-large;">&#160;</span></span>
</h2>
<h2 data-end="382" data-start="0" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: Satisfy; font-size: x-large; font-weight: normal;"><span>&#160;&quot;Fajita-bout self-control, pass the pasta&quot;</span></span>
</h2>
<h2 data-end="382" data-start="0" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Satisfy; font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: x-large;">&#160;</span></span></h2><div data-end="382" data-start="0" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjWi4MMyOHlZ5W23JPHkVTmHchEgoWx1UfE2C0dONNdBthbWHoWvihqB3PEAAX4A4D1NmHtQSjVSbfaZ6r-OvFMtLNrkSysr6yTaS3dCADzWiWbHszHdqUnGnoBcSp4psUa8IQhOEdEGIfjPQW3nLc_Vn-1NEjt634OaLasMgdXNDO3XPJdS5BfZT31rBdo/s3835/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_41.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Chicken Fajita Pasta, chicken pasta, creamy pasta, creamy chicken pasta, fajita pasta, chicken recipe, pasta, pasta recipe,  food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food flatlay, one pot recipe, meal plan, google pixel, spicy food, spicy pasta, easy pasta, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3835" data-original-width="2867" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjWi4MMyOHlZ5W23JPHkVTmHchEgoWx1UfE2C0dONNdBthbWHoWvihqB3PEAAX4A4D1NmHtQSjVSbfaZ6r-OvFMtLNrkSysr6yTaS3dCADzWiWbHszHdqUnGnoBcSp4psUa8IQhOEdEGIfjPQW3nLc_Vn-1NEjt634OaLasMgdXNDO3XPJdS5BfZT31rBdo/w478-h640/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_41.jpg" title="Chicken Fajita Pasta" width="478"></a>
    </div>
    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><br></div></span>
</div>
<div data-end="382" data-start="0" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">This <b>Chicken Fajita Pasta</b> recipe has been sitting in my drafts for
    far longer than planned. I actually made it last year, filmed everything,
    edited most of it, and then somehow it kept getting pushed further and
    further down the schedule. You know those recipes you keep telling yourself
    you&#8217;ll share &#8220;soon&#8221;? This was very much one of those.</span>
</div>
<div data-end="382" data-start="0" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
</div>
<div data-end="382" data-start="0" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjDYxAyISmB6UlKCcFmap1WoonWAMbJ-n5lKcuUqFVxri17B3voaZPx4rbxz5HMioVvjIHMmVm_eDpok2TAk1KXn9dCODnqX6NX4p_KwD68zApP2kpp3z4n4veEnQF2cWSGR33C0wIMEaN_gsLTglCS7cHq0OMlv69Sqi2BWnZiWBi1jtenxzMk6v5A_LiB/s4064/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_34.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Chicken Fajita Pasta, chicken pasta, creamy pasta, creamy chicken pasta, fajita pasta, chicken recipe, pasta, pasta recipe,  food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food flatlay, one pot recipe, meal plan, google pixel, spicy food, spicy pasta, easy pasta, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjDYxAyISmB6UlKCcFmap1WoonWAMbJ-n5lKcuUqFVxri17B3voaZPx4rbxz5HMioVvjIHMmVm_eDpok2TAk1KXn9dCODnqX6NX4p_KwD68zApP2kpp3z4n4veEnQF2cWSGR33C0wIMEaN_gsLTglCS7cHq0OMlv69Sqi2BWnZiWBi1jtenxzMk6v5A_LiB/w482-h640/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_34.jpg" title="Chicken Fajita Pasta" width="482"></a>
    </div>
    <br></span>
</div>
<div data-end="391" data-start="0" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">What I love most about this recipe is just how easy it is to make. There&#8217;s
    nothing complicated here, no fancy techniques, and no long prep time
    involved. Everything comes together quickly, which makes it perfect for busy
    weeknights when you want something comforting but still packed with flavour.&#160;</span>
</div>
<div data-end="391" data-start="0" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
</div>
<div data-end="777" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="393" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhLTBpeYVpdQYLwYltI8zwqnv1jS581oh0qnzHqzcLnncQqTqF6x7lchH9XNmjIu0BoAMf-2ceq70bB75TjZ-iK7iC60AaZesCz4oZyzAyHhYM7MIs8jdXdmPfhbPCllhHFc2HXBzhUycdNZbqexPF-v0CI16ZHKWLDapUWlbF7oV53gug01Jc2ri489CNB/s4064/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_35.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Chicken Fajita Pasta, chicken pasta, creamy pasta, creamy chicken pasta, fajita pasta, chicken recipe, pasta, pasta recipe,  food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food flatlay, one pot recipe, meal plan, google pixel, spicy food, spicy pasta, easy pasta, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhLTBpeYVpdQYLwYltI8zwqnv1jS581oh0qnzHqzcLnncQqTqF6x7lchH9XNmjIu0BoAMf-2ceq70bB75TjZ-iK7iC60AaZesCz4oZyzAyHhYM7MIs8jdXdmPfhbPCllhHFc2HXBzhUycdNZbqexPF-v0CI16ZHKWLDapUWlbF7oV53gug01Jc2ri489CNB/w482-h640/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_35.jpg" title="Chicken Fajita Pasta" width="482"></a>
    </div>
    &#160;</span>
</div>
<div data-end="777" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="393" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">I joked on my Instagram that you can turn almost any recipe into a
    &#8220;one-pot&#8221; meal if you simply skip all the steps telling you to remove
    ingredients and keep them aside, and adjust the cooking process slightly.
    This chicken fajita pasta is definitely one of those dishes you can get away
    with doing exactly that.</span></div>
<div data-end="777" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="393" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
    <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgp7Dctydyocluxd8nYZVABSES-5AVhSfaPbE75lp1V8i6AAZolUA7LWHSa_gN2vU_fP71osyuoC9NIdCbT04_25TGtNfqi7cFIeZbxyjhoEmtHZe_TzNBuGH07rOrG4LazNk2e4bmpkTYUCnsa47nScH-qqhUxOpTUaAIO2hxygojmILauGPEFxVsoXbeZ/s4064/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_32.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Chicken Fajita Pasta, chicken pasta, creamy pasta, creamy chicken pasta, fajita pasta, chicken recipe, pasta, pasta recipe,  food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food flatlay, one pot recipe, meal plan, google pixel, spicy food, spicy pasta, easy pasta, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgp7Dctydyocluxd8nYZVABSES-5AVhSfaPbE75lp1V8i6AAZolUA7LWHSa_gN2vU_fP71osyuoC9NIdCbT04_25TGtNfqi7cFIeZbxyjhoEmtHZe_TzNBuGH07rOrG4LazNk2e4bmpkTYUCnsa47nScH-qqhUxOpTUaAIO2hxygojmILauGPEFxVsoXbeZ/w482-h640/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_32.jpg" title="Chicken Fajita Pasta" width="482"></a>
  </div>
</div>
<div data-end="777" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="393" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><br></span>
</div>
<div data-end="1128" data-start="748" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">This chicken fajita pasta is also ideal for meal prep and lazy days. It
    reheats beautifully and tastes just as good the next day, if not better. You
    can make it extra saucy or keep it lightly coated depending on your
    preference, which makes it really versatile for the whole family. </span></div>
<div data-end="1128" data-start="748" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
</div>
<div data-end="1128" data-start="748" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEidA_4Qmg1kFTjQzjL6qb_hmBIsSTI_s9JQJe3F6lQcN5211oistglaj0z0LjQGDW1oiDyM38BGSSw19SRNgIZCGwQmuK038xWYcucGFbON0EJjZEE61vrL0dHRLyFCsAa8W5YeNnmxkhI4nWPewUJQ2kTq6D-imUy3vk01ifZfr_AnAp3FX19-8yTf-Z6J/s3867/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_27.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Chicken Fajita Pasta, chicken pasta, creamy pasta, creamy chicken pasta, fajita pasta, chicken recipe, pasta, pasta recipe,  food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food pictures, food flatlay, one pot recipe, meal plan, google pixel, spicy food, spicy pasta, easy pasta, food video, tiktok recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3867" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEidA_4Qmg1kFTjQzjL6qb_hmBIsSTI_s9JQJe3F6lQcN5211oistglaj0z0LjQGDW1oiDyM38BGSSw19SRNgIZCGwQmuK038xWYcucGFbON0EJjZEE61vrL0dHRLyFCsAa8W5YeNnmxkhI4nWPewUJQ2kTq6D-imUy3vk01ifZfr_AnAp3FX19-8yTf-Z6J/w506-h640/ChickenFajitaPasta_SFK_2025_27.jpg" title="Chicken Fajita Pasta" width="506"></a></div></span><br>
</div>
<div data-end="1585" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="1130" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">If you&#8217;ve been around here for a while, you&#8217;ll know I&#8217;ve already shared a
    chicken fajita recipe before, which you can click&#160;<a href="https://www.spicyfusionkitchen.com/2023/12/chicken-fajitas.html" target="_blank">here</a> for the recipe. A
    quick giggle before you scroll on, while editing the video for this pasta, I
    realised the beginning of the footage was missing, so this ended up being
    the meal I made the next day just so I could re-record the intro. Meal
    planning made easy and content creation at its finest.</span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>

  </div>

<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: Satisfy;"><span style="font-size: x-large;">&#160;</span></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: Satisfy;"><span style="font-size: x-large;">&quot;Not your average slaw. She&#8217;s sweet and spicy&quot;</span></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: Satisfy;"><span style="font-size: x-large;">&#160;&#160;</span></span>&#160;
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhJfTdh2jHiMyUUzfDQGXQGisY-1Q0jFzYC67WJUM9pNQ3YDt6EJcT_ibBrk6YCs0fb-YdOE_ixb2aUKgomMW7fI7KDPZHK0kZcgdZAshgUidqkQuu3Qkf11W8Y1WHBG6hitnLeSlFce03rVeqNk_VaxjpLXqi2KjXTCnB43PFzENW3KBqXrosZGWSiMiwd/s3043/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_24.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw, chipotle, chipotle peppers in adobo sauce, sweet potato coleslaw, sweet potato slaw, purple cabbage, purple cabbage slaw, purple cabbage coleslaw, side dish, braai, bbq, braai side dish, bbq side dish, healthy side dish, protein packed, pcos, pcos diet, food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, ramadan, food flatlay, google pixel, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3043" data-original-width="2282" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhJfTdh2jHiMyUUzfDQGXQGisY-1Q0jFzYC67WJUM9pNQ3YDt6EJcT_ibBrk6YCs0fb-YdOE_ixb2aUKgomMW7fI7KDPZHK0kZcgdZAshgUidqkQuu3Qkf11W8Y1WHBG6hitnLeSlFce03rVeqNk_VaxjpLXqi2KjXTCnB43PFzENW3KBqXrosZGWSiMiwd/w480-h640/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_24.jpg" title="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw" width="480"></a>
    </div>
    <br></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">Summer calls for light, crisp sides, and this <b>Chipotle Sweet Potato
    Coleslaw </b>ticks every box. It is vibrant, fresh and full of flavour, making
    it the perfect upgrade to your everyday coleslaw. Whether you are planning a
    casual lunch or a family gathering, this recipe brings colour and balance to
    the table.</span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><br></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
    <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgqckZrtAI_jfNhtQgjC5z9tPbNto1ORmuvD3fVxxnVM8l_TilounYHw8A8xZ-AkKzfVUs39UgFqfHXKksYwUkTdYBfGWTpAstkzGYCpIkVRBLj4AjKkHgZ8Fkcyl82Ytj56_8c75lWEcKSB8ywJUaBN3VvDcwql_39KuKMQ5BSqpRTRaEL26O7JkYIo_Vc/s4064/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_13.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw, chipotle, chipotle peppers in adobo sauce, sweet potato coleslaw, sweet potato slaw, purple cabbage, purple cabbage slaw, purple cabbage coleslaw, side dish, braai, bbq, braai side dish, bbq side dish, healthy side dish, protein packed, pcos, pcos diet, food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, ramadan, food flatlay, google pixel, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgqckZrtAI_jfNhtQgjC5z9tPbNto1ORmuvD3fVxxnVM8l_TilounYHw8A8xZ-AkKzfVUs39UgFqfHXKksYwUkTdYBfGWTpAstkzGYCpIkVRBLj4AjKkHgZ8Fkcyl82Ytj56_8c75lWEcKSB8ywJUaBN3VvDcwql_39KuKMQ5BSqpRTRaEL26O7JkYIo_Vc/w482-h640/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_13.jpg" title="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw" width="482"></a>
  </div>
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><br></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">If you follow me on social media you know how much I<i> love</i> sweet potatoes
    and purple cabbage. Sweet potatoes are packed with fibre, complex
    carbohydrates and antioxidants, making them a nourishing addition to any
    meal. Paired with crunchy purple cabbage, which is rich in vitamins C and K
    as well as powerful anthocyanins, this coleslaw is as nutritious as it is
    beautiful. Both ingredients are particularly supportive for those managing
    PCOS, helping with blood sugar balance and overall gut health.</span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><br></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
    <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiij_-Unw8zM3ZdRhZ8RP9awlHCTZdlU6SrGd1wMZjnFzH0T0OoiD8417h8SEZjR0YIdjKgnENzy4qLgVkddU2s50cdbjBF9Hw1FiXrF1Ly0PBTQqjT-Z3oOIwArNrf00KLX2eORzdtVtXgU2CIMQylTJEyMrpuZYgb1VUqHDlThFNvLpvHjsOD4RN8n4fm/s4080/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_02.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw, chipotle, chipotle peppers in adobo sauce, sweet potato coleslaw, sweet potato slaw, purple cabbage, purple cabbage slaw, purple cabbage coleslaw, side dish, braai, bbq, braai side dish, bbq side dish, healthy side dish, protein packed, pcos, pcos diet, food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, ramadan, food flatlay, google pixel, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4080" data-original-width="2994" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiij_-Unw8zM3ZdRhZ8RP9awlHCTZdlU6SrGd1wMZjnFzH0T0OoiD8417h8SEZjR0YIdjKgnENzy4qLgVkddU2s50cdbjBF9Hw1FiXrF1Ly0PBTQqjT-Z3oOIwArNrf00KLX2eORzdtVtXgU2CIMQylTJEyMrpuZYgb1VUqHDlThFNvLpvHjsOD4RN8n4fm/w470-h640/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_02.jpg" title="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw" width="470"></a>
  </div>
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><br></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">The real flavour boost comes from the <i>Chipotle Peppers in Adobo Sauce</i>,
    which add a smoky flavour without overpowering the freshness of the slaw.
    This makes it an ideal braai or BBQ side, pairing beautifully with grilled
    chicken, steak or even halloumi. It is bold enough to stand out, yet
    versatile enough to complement a wide range of mains.</span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><br></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
    <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgmfNWaWZ-H-wt_JoTp31UGlJe5Kn0zzjt6CgR22cEMU6BPuPQgdmWDy_p67yO_dXwtjhTCkFl06X2_XsS9hlUxnHg3eMNi5iWh2Bmdmdwwz9afbBoPsIpNxi_NO0r2Xb1GZDNq7K5USi0Y4j3jAePONwSAQrgpWBhmkLSknnZ278P3WpUXvw84c67T8aqp/s2340/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_20.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw, chipotle, chipotle peppers in adobo sauce, sweet potato coleslaw, sweet potato slaw, purple cabbage, purple cabbage slaw, purple cabbage coleslaw, side dish, braai, bbq, braai side dish, bbq side dish, healthy side dish, protein packed, pcos, pcos diet, food, food blog, food blogger, food photography, food video, tiktok recipe, recipe recipe, pinterest food, uk, south africa, botswana, ramadan, food flatlay, google pixel, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="2340" data-original-width="1755" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgmfNWaWZ-H-wt_JoTp31UGlJe5Kn0zzjt6CgR22cEMU6BPuPQgdmWDy_p67yO_dXwtjhTCkFl06X2_XsS9hlUxnHg3eMNi5iWh2Bmdmdwwz9afbBoPsIpNxi_NO0r2Xb1GZDNq7K5USi0Y4j3jAePONwSAQrgpWBhmkLSknnZ278P3WpUXvw84c67T8aqp/w480-h640/ChipotleSweetPotatoColeslaw_SFK_2025_20.jpg" title="Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw" width="480"></a>
  </div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><br></span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: arial;">With<b> Ramadan </b>approaching, this Chipotle Sweet Potato Coleslaw works wonderfully as a
    healthy side for iftar, offering nourishment without feeling heavy. It can
    be made ahead and stored in the fridge for up to one week, making it perfect
    for meal prep during busy summer days.&#160;</span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">&#160;</div>

<h3 style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: Satisfy; font-size: x-large; font-weight: normal;">&#160;</span><span style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: x-large;"><span style="font-family: Satisfy;">&#8220;Crispy dumpling crush, deep miso kind of love.&#8221;</span></span></span>
</h3>
<h3 style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: x-large;"><span style="font-family: Satisfy;">&#160;</span></span></span>
</h3>

    <br></span>
</div>
<div data-end="403" data-start="73" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">I&#8217;ve had these rice paper dumplings on my list to make for quite a while,
    and I finally got round to making them. After that first batch, I genuinely couldn&#8217;t stop making them they&#8217;re
    that good. They&#8217;re fun to fold, quick to cook, and the kind of recipe that
    instantly slips into your regular rotation. Stay tuned for more sauce
    recipes I plan on sharing in the future.</span>
</div>
<div data-end="403" data-start="73" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;
    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEizg-CzjJF3msGRuiXi8M7WN5-3jfiYTogt6V7WQmtlYIa7EJVUzbyBj17FoZnHG1HH_NwS_iunQ8aWTMu_0z4crbCXZLGdH-PpShevQDoPX3C7aMVKusJr4NIfv4Cddbdz0vK2exgLOqUlIAJpzbrrwbRoAskX5sFCttmn-5TqafjuE9KFdVXB8TqK0DPE/s3876/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_16.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="crispy chicken rice paper dumplings in miso sauce, miso sauce, dumpling miso sauce, miso, crispy dumplings, crispy chicken dumplings, rice paper, rice paper dumplings, crispy rice paper dumplings, spicy food, food, food photography, dumplings, food blog, food blogger, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, google pixel, crispy dumplings, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, food video, recipe video, pinterest food, food plating, food stylist, zainab dokrat, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3876" data-original-width="2907" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEizg-CzjJF3msGRuiXi8M7WN5-3jfiYTogt6V7WQmtlYIa7EJVUzbyBj17FoZnHG1HH_NwS_iunQ8aWTMu_0z4crbCXZLGdH-PpShevQDoPX3C7aMVKusJr4NIfv4Cddbdz0vK2exgLOqUlIAJpzbrrwbRoAskX5sFCttmn-5TqafjuE9KFdVXB8TqK0DPE/w480-h640/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_16.jpg" title="Crispy Chicken Rice Paper Dumplings In Miso Sauce" width="480"></a>
    </div>
    <br></span>
</div>
<div data-end="748" data-start="405" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">Rice paper dumplings are a wonderful balance of light yet crispy, and they
    come together much faster than you&#8217;d expect. The rice paper turns
    beautifully golden in the pan, giving you that satisfying crunch without
    needing complicated techniques. They&#8217;re perfect for busy days when you still
    want something fresh, homemade, and full of flavour.</span>
</div>
<div data-end="748" data-start="405" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;
    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEg4RowFCRoLOCbF7uEHJGhakGQrVrPgpuZr2Rj9Ql1lHgOCc8YXjHmWpKqmQn-ysZJC27G5BaDsrYUaLCLhqe77n09XPN4ru9lHoH6Mggl-FOK-xfVqOdE-MLUXIg1YM7flb7tasHFfdkIE8DT0JxgiW0MONaxbz4kDJzGLSN61jz4YPFWahX7baJXPyUGy/s4064/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_34.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="crispy chicken rice paper dumplings in miso sauce, miso sauce, dumpling miso sauce, miso, crispy dumplings, crispy chicken dumplings, rice paper, rice paper dumplings, crispy rice paper dumplings, spicy food, food, food photography, dumplings, food blog, food blogger, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, google pixel, crispy dumplings, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, food video, recipe video, pinterest food, food plating, food stylist, zainab dokrat, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="4064" data-original-width="3056" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEg4RowFCRoLOCbF7uEHJGhakGQrVrPgpuZr2Rj9Ql1lHgOCc8YXjHmWpKqmQn-ysZJC27G5BaDsrYUaLCLhqe77n09XPN4ru9lHoH6Mggl-FOK-xfVqOdE-MLUXIg1YM7flb7tasHFfdkIE8DT0JxgiW0MONaxbz4kDJzGLSN61jz4YPFWahX7baJXPyUGy/w482-h640/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_34.jpg" title="Crispy Chicken Rice Paper Dumplings In Miso Sauce" width="482"></a>
    </div>
    <br></span>
</div>
<div data-end="1170" data-start="750" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">The chicken filling is the real hero here. It&#8217;s flavourful, simple to
    prepare, and works as the perfect base, meaning almost any sauce you pair
    with it tastes amazing. You can also make the filling ahead of time, freeze
    it, and thaw it when needed, which makes life in the kitchen even
    easier.</span>
</div>
<div data-end="1170" data-start="750" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
</div>
<div data-end="1170" data-start="750" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgLG8z3yBQIXY9-AvSOCFESH2pS8_9HRRZr_37etF1_YYJXfw-Ro0riphxAsn6Uqn8L_6veXwyBN4of9Lc6DpR-V5C0P2XLt0GVCdhWezd1yl7ZaIDNDkHO2S4XS8pyo7B7Op4Yqk9Ni1MVAQ8IryRtuw4Rd_Cb7fjcQBQ2h7I3XDyuzG13aL0T4VI_hkYU/s3190/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_28.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="crispy chicken rice paper dumplings in miso sauce, miso sauce, dumpling miso sauce, miso, crispy dumplings, crispy chicken dumplings, rice paper, rice paper dumplings, crispy rice paper dumplings, spicy food, food, food photography, dumplings, food blog, food blogger, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, google pixel, crispy dumplings, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, food video, recipe video, pinterest food, food plating, food stylist, zainab dokrat, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3190" data-original-width="2639" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgLG8z3yBQIXY9-AvSOCFESH2pS8_9HRRZr_37etF1_YYJXfw-Ro0riphxAsn6Uqn8L_6veXwyBN4of9Lc6DpR-V5C0P2XLt0GVCdhWezd1yl7ZaIDNDkHO2S4XS8pyo7B7Op4Yqk9Ni1MVAQ8IryRtuw4Rd_Cb7fjcQBQ2h7I3XDyuzG13aL0T4VI_hkYU/w530-h640/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_28.jpg" title="Crispy Chicken Rice Paper Dumplings In Miso Sauce" width="530"></a>
    </div>
    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><br></div></span>
</div>
<div data-end="1465" data-start="1172" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">The deep miso sauce truly takes these dumplings up a level. Miso forms the
    base of the sauce and gives a lovely umami richness that pairs perfectly
    with the crispy dumpling exterior. It&#8217;s savoury, comforting, and very
    moreish, and you can easily adjust it to your taste with sweetness or
    heat. I have 2 other sauce recipes coming soon, so stay tuned for that.</span></div>
<div data-end="1465" data-start="1172" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
</div>
<div data-end="1465" data-start="1172" style="text-align: center;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
      <a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjAjbFpL0ojSh4ET_KrLb9VUp7BYKXFvRYSy2UU-uh3vBib6I1MFlPPUw9H_8QT_0Af4BhtjEpXiBbJIylrxBN9gnnGHFDTLmuvqwN_FzChsN0cOg196ZLkpO_bUyOIwTVvrCPntTgSjVuSiA6mq5-yIwW5cJjmDWoqjM8OheYWZ5eEbLGv-LQ7C_ItKm-S/s3899/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_13.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" title=""><img alt="crispy chicken rice paper dumplings in miso sauce, miso sauce, dumpling miso sauce, miso, crispy dumplings, crispy chicken dumplings, rice paper, rice paper dumplings, crispy rice paper dumplings, spicy food, food, food photography, dumplings, food blog, food blogger, food flatlay, uk, south africa, botswana, google pixel, crispy dumplings, tiktok recipe, recipe reel, food video, recipe video, pinterest food, food plating, food stylist, zainab dokrat, spicy fusion kitchen" border="0" data-original-height="3899" data-original-width="2924" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjAjbFpL0ojSh4ET_KrLb9VUp7BYKXFvRYSy2UU-uh3vBib6I1MFlPPUw9H_8QT_0Af4BhtjEpXiBbJIylrxBN9gnnGHFDTLmuvqwN_FzChsN0cOg196ZLkpO_bUyOIwTVvrCPntTgSjVuSiA6mq5-yIwW5cJjmDWoqjM8OheYWZ5eEbLGv-LQ7C_ItKm-S/w480-h640/CrispyChickenDumplingsInMisoSauce_SFK_2025_13.jpg" title="Crispy Chicken Rice Paper Dumplings In Miso Sauce" width="480"></a>
    </div>
    <br></span>
</div>
<div data-end="1837" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="" data-start="1467" style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">These dumplings are also freezer-friendly. You can freeze the filling on
    its own, or assemble the dumplings and freeze them uncooked. Simply freeze
    them in a single layer first, then transfer to a container, and cook
    straight from frozen when you&#8217;re ready. <b>This recipe yeilds approximately 24 dumplings.&#160;</b></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
  <span style="font-family: arial;">&#160;</span>

<script type='text/javascript'>//<![CDATA[
$(document).ready(function() {
  // change the dimension variable below to be the pixel size you want

  // this identifies the PopularPosts1 div element, finds each image in it, and resizes it
  $('.post-image').find('img').each(function(n, image){
    var image = $(image);
image.attr({src : image.attr('src').replace("s72", "s1600")});
image.attr({src : image.attr('src').replace("s320", "s1600")});
image.attr({src : image.attr('src').replace("s400", "s1600")});
